Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.

Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.

Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.

Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.

Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.
Sony Xperia 1 III
Thit b Xperia cao cp ca Sony ni ting vi mn hnh OLED 4K, camera mnh m vi quang hc Zeiss, v kh nng m thanh xut sc.

in thoi c th gp c o t Samsung cung cp mt mn hnh ln c th gp, h tr S Pen, v mt thit k cao cp.

Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.
Sony Xperia 1 III

OnePlus Nord 2
Mt sn phm tm trung t OnePlus vi s tp trung vo tri nghim ngi dng mt m, hiu sut camera kh, v kt ni 5G.
Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 3

Google Pixel 5a

iPhone 13 Pro
Mt chic in thoi thng minh mnh m v y  tnh nng t Apple. Trang b vi x l A15 Bionic mi nht, mn hnh ProMotion, v h thng camera tin tin.
Samsung Galaxy S21
in thoi Android cao cp ca Samsung vi mt mn hnh p, vi x l mnh m Exynos/Snapdragon, v h thng camera a dng.
Google Pixel 6
Thit b Pixel mi nht ca Google vi mt camera tuyt vi s dng cng ngh chp nh tnh ton, tri nghim Android thun ty, v hiu sut nhanh chng.
OnePlus 9
in thoi cao cp t OnePlus, ni ting vi giao din OxygenOS mt m, sc nhanh, v s hp tc vi Hasselblad cho ti u ha camera.
Xiaomi Mi 11
Mt chic flagship gi phi chng t Xiaomi, cung cp vi x l Snapdragon, mn hnh vi tc  lm mi cao, v h thng camera a dng.
Huawei P50 Pro
in thoi cao cp ca Huawei vi h thng camera mnh m, vi x l Kirin tin tin, v thit k thanh lch.
Sony Xperia 1 III
Thit b Xperia cao cp ca Sony ni ting vi mn hnh OLED 4K, camera mnh m vi quang hc Zeiss, v kh nng m thanh xut sc.
OnePlus Nord 2
Mt sn phm tm trung t OnePlus vi s tp trung vo tri nghim ngi dng mt m, hiu sut camera kh, v kt ni 5G.
Samsung Galaxy Z Fold 3
in thoi c th gp c o t Samsung cung cp mt mn hnh ln c th gp, h tr S Pen, v mt thit k cao cp.
Google Pixel 5a
Sn phm Pixel gi r ca Google vi s tp trung vo cht lng camera, Android gc v pin lu di.
